and ARKStep stepper modules. This is based on a new set of shared classes, `SUNAdjointStepper` and `SUNAdjointCheckpointScheme`. A new example demonstrating this capability can be found in `examples/arkode/C_serial/ark_lotka_volterra_ASA.c`.\r\n\r\n### New Features and Enhancements\r\n\r\n#### ARKODE\r\n\r\nThe following changes have been made to the default ERK, DIRK, and ARK methods in ARKODE to utilize more efficient methods:\r\n\r\n| Type               | Old Default                                                      | New Default                                                        |\r\n| ------------------ | ---------------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------ |\r\n| 2nd Order Explicit | `ARKODE_HEUN_EULER_2_1_2`                                        | `ARKODE_RALSTON_3_1_2`                                             |\r\n| 4th Order Explicit | `ARKODE_ZONNEVELD_5_3_4`                                         | `ARKODE_SOFRONIOU_SPALETTA_5_3_4`                                  |\r\n| 5th Order Explicit | `ARKODE_CASH_KARP_6_4_5`                                         | `ARKODE_TSITOURAS_7_4_5`                                           |\r\n| 6th Order Explicit | `ARKODE_VERNER_8_5_6`                                            | `ARKODE_VERNER_9_5_6`                                              |\r\n| 8th Order Explicit | `ARKODE_FEHLBERG_13_7_8`                                         | `ARKODE_VERNER_13_7_8`                                             |\r\n| 2nd Order Implicit | `ARKODE_SDIRK_2_1_2`                                             | `ARKODE_ARK2_DIRK_3_1_2`                                           |\r\n| 3rd Order Implicit | `ARKODE_ARK324L2SA_DIRK_4_2_3`                                   | `ARKODE_ESDIRK325L2SA_5_2_3`                                       |\r\n| 4th Order Implicit | `ARKODE_SDIRK_5_3_4`                                             | `ARKODE_ESDIRK436L2SA_6_3_4`                                       |\r\n| 5th Order Implicit | `ARKODE_ARK548L2SA_DIRK_8_4_5`                                   | `ARKODE_ESDIRK547L2SA2_7_4_5`                                      |\r\n| 4th Order ARK      | `ARKODE_ARK436L2SA_ERK_6_3_4` and `ARKODE_ARK436L2SA_DIRK_6_3_4` | `ARKODE_ARK437L2SA_ERK_7_3_4` and `ARKODE_ARK437L2SA_DIRK_7_3_4`   |\r\n| 5th Order ARK      | `ARKODE_ARK548L2SA_ERK_8_4_5` and `ARKODE_ARK548L2SA_DIRK_8_4_5` | `ARKODE_ARK548L2SAb_ERK_8_4_5` and `ARKODE_ARK548L2SAb_DIRK_8_4_5` |\r\n\r\n\r\nThe old default methods can be loaded using the functions `ERKStepSetTableName` or `ERKStepSetTableNum` with ERKStep and `ARKStepSetTableName` or `ARKStepSetTableNum` with ARKStep and passing the desired method name string or constant, respectively. For example, the following call can be used to load the old default fourth order method with ERKStep:\r\n```\r\n/* Load the old 4th order ERK method using the table name */\r\nierr = ERKStepSetTableName(arkode_mem, \"ARKODE_ZONNEVELD_5_3_4\");\r\n```\r\nSimilarly with ARKStep, the following calls can be used for ERK, DIRK, or ARK\r\nmethods, respectively:\r\n```\r\n/* Load the old 4th order ERK method by name */\r\nierr = ARKStepSetTableName(arkode_mem, \"ARKODE_DIRK_NONE\", \"ARKODE_ZONNEVELD_5_3_4\");\r\n\r\n/* Load the old 4th order DIRK method by name */\r\nierr = ARKStepSetTableName(arkode_mem, \"ARKODE_SDIRK_5_3_4\", \"ARKODE_ERK_NONE\");\r\n\r\n/* Load the old 4th order ARK method by name */\r\nierr = ARKStepSetTableName(arkode_mem, \"ARKODE_ARK436L2SA_DIRK_6_3_4\", \"ARKODE_ARK436L2SA_ERK_6_3_4\");\r\n```\r\n\r\nAdditionally, the following changes have been made to the default time step adaptivity parameters in ARKODE:\r\n\r\n| Parameter             | Old Default           | New Default |\r\n|-----------------------|-----------------------|-------------|\r\n| Controller            | PID (PI for ERKStep)  | I           |\r\n| Safety Factor         | 0.96                  | 0.9         |\r\n| Bias                  | 1.5 (1.2 for ERKStep) | 1.0         |\r\n| Fixed Step Bounds     | [1.0, 1.5]            | [1.0, 1.0]  |\r\n| Adaptivity Adjustment | -1                    | 0           |\r\n\r\nThe following calls can be used to restore the old defaults for ERKStep:\r\n```\r\nSUNAdaptController controller = SUNAdaptController_Soderlind(ctx);\r\nSUNAdaptController_SetParams_PI(controller, 0.8, -0.31);\r\nARKodeSetAdaptController(arkode_mem, controller);\r\nSUNAdaptController_SetErrorBias(controller, 1.2);\r\nARKodeSetSafetyFactor(arkode_mem, 0.96);\r\nARKodeSetFixedStepBounds(arkode_mem, 1, 1.5);\r\nARKodeSetAdaptivityAdjustment(arkode_mem, -1);\r\n```\r\nThe following calls can be used to restore the old defaults for other ARKODE integrators:\r\n```\r\nSUNAdaptController controller = SUNAdaptController_PID(ctx);\r\nARKodeSetAdaptController(arkode_mem, controller);\r\nSUNAdaptController_SetErrorBias(controller, 1.5);\r\nARKodeSetSafetyFactor(arkode_mem, 0.96);\r\nARKodeSetFixedStepBounds(arkode_mem, 1, 1.5);\r\nARKodeSetAdaptivityAdjustment(arkode_mem, -1);\r\n```\r\nIn both cases above, destroy the controller at the end of the run with `SUNAdaptController_Destroy(controller);`.\r\n\r\nThe Soderlind time step adaptivity controller now starts with an I controller until there is sufficient history of past time steps and errors.\r\n\r\nAdded `ARKodeSetAdaptControllerByName` to set a time step adaptivity controller with a string. There are also four new controllers: `SUNAdaptController_H0211`, `SUNAdaptController_H0321`, `SUNAdaptController_H211`, and `SUNAdaptController_H312`.\r\n\r\nAdded the `ARKODE_RALSTON_3_1_2` and `ARKODE_TSITOURAS_7_4_5` explicit Runge-Kutta Butcher tables.\r\n\r\nImproved the precision of the coefficients for `ARKODE_ARK324L2SA_ERK_4_2_3`, `ARKODE_VERNER_9_5_6`, `ARKODE_VERNER_10_6_7`, `ARKODE_VERNER_13_7_8`, `ARKODE_ARK324L2SA_DIRK_4_2_3`, and `ARKODE_ESDIRK324L2SA_4_2_3`.\r\n\r\n#### CVODE / CVODES\r\n\r\nAdded support for resizing CVODE and CVODES when solving initial value problems where the number of equations and unknowns changes over time. Resizing requires a user supplied history of solution and right-hand side values at the new problem size, see `CVodeResizeHistory` for more information.\r\n\r\n#### KINSOL\r\n\r\nAdded support in KINSOL for setting user-supplied functions to compute the damping factor and, when using Anderson acceleration, the depth in fixed-point or Picard iterations. See `KINSetDampingFn` and `KINSetDepthFn`, respectively, for more information.\r\n\r\n#### SUNDIALS Types\r\n\r\nA new type, `suncountertype`, was added for the integer type used for counter variables. It is currently an alias for `long int`.\r\n\r\n### Bug Fixes\r\n\r\n#### ARKODE\r\n\r\nFixed bug in `ARKodeResize` which caused it return an error for MRI methods.\r\n\r\nRemoved error floors from the `SUNAdaptController` implementations which could unnecessarily limit the time size growth, particularly after the first step.\r\n\r\nFixed bug in `ARKodeSetFixedStep` where it could return `ARK_SUCCESS` despite an error occurring.\r\n\r\nFixed bug in the ARKODE SPRKStep `SPRKStepReInit` function and `ARKodeReset` function with SPRKStep that could cause a segmentation fault when compensated summation is not used.\r\n\r\n#### KINSOL\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in KINSOL where an incorrect damping parameter is applied on the initial iteration with Anderson acceleration unless `KINSetDamping` and `KINSetDampingAA` are both called with the same value when enabling damping.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in KINSOL where errors that occurred when computing Anderson acceleration were not captured.\r\n\r\nAdded missing return values to `KINGetReturnFlagName`.\r\n\r\n#### CMake\r\n\r\nFixed the behavior of `SUNDIALS_ENABLE_ERROR_CHECKS` so additional runtime error checks are disabled by default with all release build types. Previously, `MinSizeRel` builds enabled additional error checking by default.\r\n\r\n### Deprecation Notices\r\n\r\nAll work space functions, e.g., `CVodeGetWorkSpace` and `ARKodeGetLinWorkSpace`, have been deprecated and will be removed in version 8.0.0."}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/191912878", "assets_url": "browser_download_url": "https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/releases/download/v7.2.0/sundials-7.2.0.tar.gz"}], "tarball_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/tarball/v7.2.0", "zipball_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v7.2.0", "body": "### Major Features\r\n\r\nAdded a time-stepping module to ARKODE for low storage Runge--Kutta methods, LSRKStep.  This currently supports five explicit low-storage methods: the second-order Runge--Kutta--Chebyshev and Runge--Kutta--Legendre methods, and the second- through fourth-order optimal strong stability preserving Runge--Kutta methods. All methods include embeddings for temporal adaptivity.\r\n\r\nAdded an operator splitting module, SplittingStep, and forcing method module, ForcingStep, to ARKODE. These modules support a broad range of operator-split time integration methods for multiphysics applications.\r\n\r\nAdded support for multirate time step adaptivity controllers, based on the recently introduced `SUNAdaptController` base class, to ARKODE's MRIStep module. As a part of this, we added embeddings for existing MRI-GARK methods, as well as support for embedded MERK and IMEX-MRI-SR methods. Added new default MRI methods for temporally adaptive versus fixed-step runs.\r\n\r\n### New Features and Enhancements\r\n\r\n#### Logging\r\n\r\nThe information level logging output in ARKODE, CVODE(S), and IDA(S) has been updated to be more uniform across the packages and a new `tools` directory has been added with a Python module, `suntools`, containing utilities for parsing logging output. The Python utilities for parsing CSV output have been relocated from the `scripts` directory to the Python module.\r\n\r\n#### SUNStepper\r\n\r\nAdded the `SUNStepper` base class to represent a generic solution procedure for IVPs. This is used by the SplittingStep and ForcingStep modules of ARKODE. A SUNStepper can be created from an ARKODE memory block with the new function `ARKodeCreateSUNStepper`. To enable interoperability with `MRIStepInnerStepper`, the function `MRIStepInnerStepper_CreateFromSUNStepper` was added.\r\n\r\n#### ARKODE\r\n\r\nAdded functionality to ARKODE to accumulate a temporal error estimate over multiple time steps. See the routines `ARKodeSetAccumulatedErrorType`, `ARKodeResetAccumulatedError`, and `ARKodeGetAccumulatedError` for details.\r\n\r\nAdded the `ARKodeSetStepDirection` and `ARKodeGetStepDirection` functions to change and query the direction of integration.\r\n\r\nAdded the function `MRIStepGetNumInnerStepperFails` to retrieve the number of recoverable failures reported by the MRIStepInnerStepper.\r\n\r\nAdded a utility routine to wrap any valid ARKODE integrator for use as an MRIStep inner stepper object, `ARKodeCreateMRIStepInnerStepper`.\r\n\r\nThe following DIRK schemes now have coefficients accurate to quad precision:\r\n* `ARKODE_BILLINGTON_3_3_2`\r\n* `ARKODE_KVAERNO_4_2_3`\r\n* `ARKODE_CASH_5_2_4`\r\n* `ARKODE_CASH_5_3_4`\r\n* `ARKODE_KVAERNO_5_3_4`\r\n* `ARKODE_KVAERNO_7_4_5`\r\n\r\n#### CMake\r\n\r\nThe default value of `CMAKE_CUDA_ARCHITECTURES` is no longer set to `70` and is now determined automatically by CMake. The previous default was only valid for Volta GPUs while the automatically selected value will vary across compilers and compiler versions. As such, users are encouraged to override this value with the architecture for their system.\r\n\r\nThe build system has been updated to utilize the CMake LAPACK imported target which should ease building SUNDIALS with LAPACK libraries that require setting specific linker flags e.g., MKL.\r\n\r\n#### Third Party Libraries\r\n\r\nThe Trilinos Teptra NVector interface has been updated to utilize CMake imported targets added in Trilinos 14 to improve support for different Kokkos backends with Trilinos. As such, Trilinos 14 or newer is required and the `Trilinos_INTERFACE_*` CMake options have been removed.\r\n\r\nExample programs using *hypre* have been updated to support v2.20 and newer.\r\n\r\n### Bug Fixes\r\n\r\n#### CMake\r\n\r\nFixed a CMake bug regarding usage of missing \"print_warning\" macro that was only triggered when the deprecated `CUDA_ARCH` option was used.\r\n\r\nFixed a CMake configuration issue related to aliasing an `ALIAS` target when using `ENABLE_KLU=ON` in combination with a static-only build of SuiteSparse.\r\n\r\nFixed a CMake issue which caused third-party CMake variables to be unset.  Users may see more options in the CMake GUI now as a result of the fix.  See details in GitHub Issue [#538](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/538).\r\n\r\n#### NVector\r\n\r\nFixed a build failure with the SYCL NVector when using Intel oneAPI 2025.0 compilers. See GitHub Issue [#596](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/596).\r\n\r\nFixed compilation errors when building the Trilinos Teptra NVector with CUDA support.\r\n\r\n#### SUNMatrix\r\n\r\nFixed a [bug](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/581) in the sparse matrix implementation of `SUNMatScaleAddI` which caused out of bounds writes unless `indexvals` were in ascending order for each row/column.\r\n\r\n#### SUNLinearSolver\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in the SPTFQMR linear solver where recoverable preconditioner errors were reported as unrecoverable.\r\n\r\n#### ARKODE\r\n\r\nFixed `ARKodeResize` not using the default `hscale` when an argument of `0` was provided.\r\n\r\nFixed a memory leak that could occur if ``ARKodeSetDefaults`` is called repeatedly.\r\n\r\nFixed the loading of ARKStep's default first order explicit method.\r\n\r\nFixed loading the default IMEX-MRI method if `ARKodeSetOrder` is used to specify a third or fourth order method. Previously, the default second order method was loaded in both cases.\r\n\r\nFixed potential memory leaks and out of bounds array accesses that could occur in the ARKODE Lagrange interpolation module when changing the method order or polynomial degree after re-initializing an integrator.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in ARKODE when enabling rootfinding with fixed step sizes and the initial value of the rootfinding function is zero. In this case, uninitialized right-hand side data was used to compute a state value near the initial condition to determine if any rootfinding functions are initially active.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in MRIStep where the data supplied to the Hermite interpolation module did not include contributions from the fast right-hand side function. With this fix, users will see one additional fast right-hand side function evaluation per slow step with the Hermite interpolation option.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in SPRKStep when using compensated summations where the error vector was not initialized to zero.\r\n\r\n#### CVODE(S)\r\n\r\nFixed a bug where `CVodeSetProjFailEta` would ignore the `eta` parameter.\r\n\r\n#### Fortran Interfaces\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in the 32-bit ``sunindextype`` Fortran interfaces to ``N_VGetSubvectorArrayPointer_ManyVector``, ``N_VGetSubvectorArrayPointer_MPIManyVector``, ``SUNBandMatrix_Column`` and ``SUNDenseMatrix_Column`` where 64-bit ``sunindextype`` interface functions were used.\r\n\r\n### Deprecation Notices\r\n\r\nDeprecated the ARKStep-specific utility routine for wrapping an ARKStep instance as an MRIStep inner stepper object, `ARKStepCreateMRIStepInnerStepper`. Use `ARKodeCreateMRIStepInnerStepper` instead.\r\n\r\nThe ARKODE stepper specific functions to retrieve the number of right-hand side function evaluations have been deprecated. Use `ARKodeGetNumRhsEvals` instead.", "reactions": {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/190286009/reactions", "total_count": 3, "+1": 0, "-1": 0, "laugh": 0, "hooray": 3, "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v7.1.0", "body": "### Major Features\r\n\r\nCreated shared user interface functions for ARKODE to allow more uniform control over time-stepping algorithms, improved extensibility, and simplified code maintenance. The corresponding stepper-specific user-callable functions are now deprecated and will be removed in a future major release.\r\n\r\nAdded CMake infrastructure that enables externally maintained addons/plugins to be *optionally* built with SUNDIALS. See the [Contributing Guide](./CONTRIBUTING.md) for more details.\r\n\r\n### New Features and Enhancements\r\n\r\nAdded support for Kokkos Kernels v4.\r\n\r\nAdded the following Runge-Kutta Butcher tables\r\n* `ARKODE_FORWARD_EULER_1_1`\r\n* `ARKODE_RALSTON_EULER_2_1_2`\r\n* `ARKODE_EXPLICIT_MIDPOINT_EULER_2_1_2`\r\n* `ARKODE_BACKWARD_EULER_1_1`\r\n* `ARKODE_IMPLICIT_MIDPOINT_1_2`\r\n* `ARKODE_IMPLICIT_TRAPEZOIDAL_2_2`\r\n\r\nAdded the following MRI coupling tables\r\n* `ARKODE_MRI_GARK_FORWARD_EULER`\r\n* `ARKODE_MRI_GARK_RALSTON2`\r\n* `ARKODE_MRI_GARK_RALSTON3`\r\n* `ARKODE_MRI_GARK_BACKWARD_EULER`\r\n* `ARKODE_MRI_GARK_IMPLICIT_MIDPOINT`\r\n* `ARKODE_IMEX_MRI_GARK_EULER`\r\n* `ARKODE_IMEX_MRI_GARK_TRAPEZOIDAL`\r\n* `ARKODE_IMEX_MRI_GARK_MIDPOINT`\r\n\r\nAdded `ARKodeButcherTable_ERKIDToName` and `ARKodeButcherTable_DIRKIDToName` to convert a Butcher table ID to a string representation.\r\n\r\nAdded the function ``ARKodeSetAutonomous`` in ARKODE to indicate that the implicit right-hand side function does not explicitly depend on time. When using the trivial predictor, an autonomous problem may reuse implicit function evaluations across stage solves to reduce the total number of function evaluations.\r\n\r\nUsers may now disable interpolated output in ARKODE by passing `ARK_INTERP_NONE` to `ARKodeSetInterpolantType`. When interpolation is disabled, rootfinding is not supported, implicit methods must use the trivial predictor (the default option), and interpolation at stop times cannot be used (interpolating at stop times is disabled by default). With interpolation disabled, calling `ARKodeEvolve` in `ARK_NORMAL` mode will return at or past the requested output time (setting a stop time may still be used to halt the integrator at a specific time). Disabling interpolation will reduce the memory footprint of an integrator by two or more state vectors (depending on the interpolant type and degree) which can be beneficial when interpolation is not needed e.g., when integrating to a final time without output in between or using an explicit fast time scale integrator with an MRI method.\r\n\r\nAdded \"Resize\" capability to ARKODE's SPRKStep time-stepping module.\r\n\r\nEnabled the Fortran interfaces to build with 32-bit `sunindextype`.\r\n\r\n### Bug Fixes\r\n\r\nUpdated the CMake variable `HIP_PLATFORM` default to `amd` as the previous default, `hcc`, is no longer recognized in ROCm 5.7.0 or newer. The new default is also valid in older version of ROCm (at least back to version 4.3.1).\r\n\r\nRenamed the DPCPP value for the `SUNDIALS_GINKGO_BACKENDS` CMake option to `SYCL` to match Ginkgo's updated naming convention.\r\n\r\nChanged the CMake version compatibility mode for SUNDIALS to `AnyNewerVersion` instead of `SameMajorVersion`. This fixes the issue seen [here](https://github.com/AMReX-Codes/amrex/pull/3835).\r\n\r\nFixed a CMake bug that caused an MPI linking error for our C++ examples in some instances. Fixes [GitHub Issue #464](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/464).\r\n\r\nFixed the runtime library installation path for windows systems. This fix changes the default library installation path from\r\n`CMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX/CMAKE_INSTALL_LIBDIR` to `CMAKE_INSTALL_PREFIX/CMAKE_INSTALL_BINDIR`.\r\n\r\nFixed conflicting `.lib` files between shared and static libs when using `MSVC` on Windows.\r\n\r\nFixed invalid `SUNDIALS_EXPORT` generated macro when building both shared and static libs.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in some Fortran examples where `c_null_ptr` was passed as an argument to a function pointer instead of `c_null_funptr`. This caused compilation issues with the Cray Fortran compiler.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in the HIP execution policies where `WARP_SIZE` would not be set with ROCm 6.0.0 or newer.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug that caused error messages to be cut off in some cases. Fixes [GitHub Issue #461](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/461).\r\n\r\nFixed a memory leak when an error handler was added to a `SUNContext`. Fixes [GitHub Issue #466](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/466).\r\n\r\nFixed a bug where `MRIStepEvolve` would not handle a recoverable error produced from evolving the inner stepper.\r\n\r\nAdded missing `SetRootDirection` and `SetNoInactiveRootWarn` functions to ARKODE's SPRKStep time-stepping module.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in `ARKodeSPRKTable_Create` where the coefficient arrays were not allocated.\r\n\r\nFix bug on LLP64 platforms (like Windows 64-bit) where `KLU_INDEXTYPE` could be 32 bits wide even if `SUNDIALS_INT64_T` is defined.\r\n\r\nCheck if size of `SuiteSparse_long` is 8 if the size of `sunindextype` is 8 when using KLU.\r\n\r\nFixed several build errors with the Fortran interfaces on Windows systems.\r\n\r\n### Deprecation Notices\r\n\r\nNumerous ARKODE stepper-specific functions are now deprecated in favor of ARKODE-wide functions.\r\n\r\nDeprecated the `ARKStepSetOptimalParams` function. Since this function does not have an ARKODE-wide equivalent, instructions have been added to the user guide for how to retain the current functionality using other user-callable functions.\r\n\r\nThe unsupported implementations of `N_VGetArrayPointer` and `N_VSetArrayPointer` for the *hypre* and PETSc vectors are now deprecated.  Users should access the underlying wrapped external library vector objects instead with `N_VGetVector_ParHyp` and `N_VGetVector_Petsc`, respectively."}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v7.0.0", "body": "### Major Feature\r\n\r\nSUNDIALS now has more robust and uniform error handling. Non-release builds will be built with additional error checking by default. See the [Error Checking](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/latest/sundials/Errors_link.html) section in the user guide for details.\r\n\r\n### Breaking Changes\r\n\r\n#### Minimum C Standard\r\n\r\nSUNDIALS now requires using a compiler that supports a subset of the C99 standard. Note with the Microsoft C/C++ compiler the subset of C99 features utilized by SUNDIALS are available starting with [Visual Studio 2015](https://learn.microsoft.com/en-us/cpp/overview/visual-cpp-language-conformance?view=msvc-170#c-standard-library-features-1).\r\n\r\n#### Deprecated Types and Functions Removed\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated types `realtype` and `booleantype` were removed from `sundials_types.h` and replaced with `sunrealtype` and `sunbooleantype`. The deprecated names for these types can be used by including the header file `sundials_types_deprecated.h` but will be fully removed in the next major release. Functions, types and header files that were previously deprecated have also been removed.\r\n\r\n#### Error Handling Changes\r\n\r\nWith the addition of the new error handling capability, the `*SetErrHandlerFn` and `*SetErrFile` functions in CVODE(S), IDA(S), ARKODE, and KINSOL have been removed. Users of these functions can use the functions `SUNContext_PushErrHandler`, and `SUNLogger_SetErrorFilename` instead. For further details see the [Error Checking](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/latest/sundials/Errors_link.html) and [Logging](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/latest/sundials/Logging_link.html) sections in the documentation.\r\n\r\nIn addition the following names/symbols were replaced by ``SUN_ERR_*`` codes:\r\n\r\n| Removed                                                    | Replaced with ``SUNErrCode``         |\r\n|:--------------------------------------------------------|:------------------------------------------------|\r\n| `SUNLS_SUCCESS`                                  | `SUN_SUCCESS`                             |\r\n| `SUNLS_UNRECOV_FAILURE`                 | no replacement (value was unused) |\r\n| `SUNLS_MEM_NULL`                                | `SUN_ERR_ARG_CORRUPT`         |\r\n| `SUNLS_ILL_INPUT`                                  | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                         |\r\n| `SUNLS_MEM_FAIL`                                  | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                  |\r\n| `SUNLS_PACKAGE_FAIL_UNREC`           | `SUN_ERR_EXT_FAIL`                   |\r\n| `SUNLS_VECTOROP_ERR`                      | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                     |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_SUCCESS`                              | `SUN_SUCCESS`                            |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_MEM_NULL`                            | `SUN_ERR_ARG_CORRUPT`        |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_MEM_FAIL`                              | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                 |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_ILL_INPUT`                              | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                        |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_VECTOROP_ERR`                  | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                     |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_EXT_FAIL`                               | `SUN_ERR_EXT_FAIL`                   |\r\n| `SUNMAT_SUCCESS`                                | `SUN_SUCCESS`                           |\r\n| `SUNMAT_ILL_INPUT`                                | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                       |\r\n| `SUNMAT_MEM_FAIL`                                | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                |\r\n| `SUNMAT_OPERATION_FAIL`                    | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                   |\r\n| `SUNMAT_MATVEC_SETUP_REQUIRED` | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                   |\r\n\r\nThe following functions have had their signature updated to ensure they can leverage the new SUNDIALS error handling capabilities.\r\n\r\n```c\r\n// From sundials_futils.h\r\nSUNDIALSFileOpen\r\nSUNDIALSFileClose\r\n\r\n// From sundials_memory.h\r\nSUNMemorNewEmpty\r\nSUNMemoryHelper_Alias\r\nSUNMemoryHelper_Wrap\r\n\r\n// From sundials_nvector.h\r\nN_VNewVectorArray\r\n```\r\n\r\n#### SUNComm Type Added\r\n\r\nWe have replaced the use of a type-erased (i.e., `void*`) pointer to a communicator in place of `MPI_Comm` throughout the SUNDIALS API with a `SUNComm`, which is just a typedef to an `int` in builds without MPI and a typedef to a `MPI_Comm` in builds with MPI. As a result:\r\n\r\n- All users will need to update their codes because the call to  `SUNContext_Create` now takes a `SUNComm` instead  of type-erased pointer to a communicator. For non-MPI codes,  pass `SUN_COMM_NULL` to the `comm` argument instead of  `NULL`. For MPI codes, pass the `MPI_Comm` directly.\r\n\r\n- The same change must be made for calls to `SUNLogger_Create` or `SUNProfiler_Create`.\r\n\r\n- Some users will need to update their calls to `N_VGetCommunicator`, and update any custom `N_Vector` implementations that provide `N_VGetCommunicator`, since it now returns a `SUNComm`.\r\n\r\nThe change away from type-erased pointers for `SUNComm` fixes problems like the one described in [GitHub Issue #275](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/275).\r\n\r\nThe SUNLogger is now always MPI-aware if MPI is enabled in SUNDIALS and the `SUNDIALS_LOGGING_ENABLE_MPI` CMake option and macro definition were removed accordingly.\r\n\r\n#### SUNDIALS Core Library\r\n\r\nUsers now need to link to `sundials_core` in addition to the libraries already linked to. This will be picked up automatically in projects that use the SUNDIALS CMake target. The library `sundials_generic` has been superseded by `sundials_core` and is no longer available. This fixes some duplicate symbol errors on Windows when linking to multiple SUNDIALS libraries.\r\n\r\n#### Fortran Interface Modules Streamlined\r\n\r\nWe have streamlined the Fortran modules that need to be included by users by combining the SUNDIALS core into one Fortran module, `fsundials_core_mod`. Modules for implementations of the core APIs still exist (e.g., for the Dense linear solver there is `fsunlinsol_dense_mod`) as do the modules for the SUNDIALS packages (e.g., `fcvode_mod`). The following modules are the ones that have been consolidated into `fsundials_core_mod`:\r\n\r\n```\r\nfsundials_adaptcontroller_mod\r\nfsundials_context_mod\r\nfsundials_futils_mod\r\nfsundials_linearsolver_mod\r\nfsundials_logger_mod\r\nfsundials_matrix_mod\r\nfsundials_nonlinearsolver_mod\r\nfsundials_nvector_mod\r\nfsundials_profiler_mod\r\nfsundials_types_mod\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Deprecation notice\r\n\r\nThe functions in `sundials_math.h` will be deprecated in the next release.\r\n\r\n```c\r\n  sunrealtype SUNRpowerI(sunrealtype base, int exponent);\r\n  sunrealtype SUNRpowerR(sunrealtype base, sunrealtype exponent);\r\n  sunbooleantype SUNRCompare(sunrealtype a, sunrealtype b);\r\n  sunbooleantype SUNRCompareTol(sunrealtype a, sunrealtype b, sunrealtype tol);\r\n  sunrealtype SUNStrToReal(const char* str);\r\n```\r\n\r\nAdditionally, the following header files (and everything in them) will be\r\ndeprecated -- users who rely on these are recommended to transition to the\r\ncorresponding `SUNMatrix` and `SUNLinearSolver` modules:\r\n\r\n```c\r\nsundials_direct.h\r\nsundials_dense.h\r\nsundials_band.h\r\n```\r\n\r\n### Minor Changes\r\n\r\nFixed [#329](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/329) so that C++20 aggregate initialization can be used.\r\n\r\nFixed integer overflow in the internal SUNDIALS hashmap. This resolves [#409](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/409) and [#249](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/249).\r\n\r\nThe `CMAKE_BUILD_TYPE` defaults to `RelWithDebInfo` mode now i.e., SUNDIALS will be built with optimizations and debugging symbols enabled by default. Previously the build type was unset by default so no optimization or debugging flags were set.\r\n\r\nThe advanced CMake options to override the inferred LAPACK name-mangling scheme have been updated from `SUNDIALS_F77_FUNC_CASE` and `SUNDIALS_F77_FUNC_UNDERSCORES` to `SUNDIALS_LAPACK_CASE` and `SUNDIALS_LAPACK_UNDERSCORES`, respectively.\r\n\r\nConverted most previous Fortran 77 and 90 examples to use SUNDIALS' Fortran 2003 interface."}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/135723888", "assets_url": "zipball_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v7.0.0-rc.1", "body": "\u26a0\ufe0f This is a release candidate.\r\n\r\n### Major Feature\r\n\r\nSUNDIALS now has more robust and uniform error handling. Non-release builds will be built with additional error checking by default. See the [Error Checking](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/v7.0.0-rc.1/sundials/Errors_link.html) section in the user guide for details.\r\n\r\n### Breaking Changes\r\n\r\n#### Deprecated Types and Functions Removed\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated types `realtype` and `booleantype` were removed from `sundials_types.h` and replaced with `sunrealtype` and `sunbooleantype`. The deprecated names for these types can be used by including the header file `sundials_types_deprecated.h` but will be fully removed in the next major release. Functions, types and header files that were previously deprecated have also been removed.\r\n\r\n#### Error Handling Changes\r\n\r\nWith the addition of the new error handling capability, the `*SetErrHandlerFn` and `*SetErrFile` functions in CVODE(S), IDA(S), ARKODE, and KINSOL have been removed. Users of these functions can use the functions `SUNContext_PushErrHandler`, and `SUNLogger_SetErrorFilename` instead. For further details see the [Error Checking](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/v7.0.0-rc.1/sundials/Errors_link.html) and [Logging](https://sundials.readthedocs.io/en/v7.0.0-rc.1/sundials/Logging_link.html) sections in the documentation.\r\n\r\nIn addition the following names/symbols were replaced by ``SUN_ERR_*`` codes:\r\n\r\n| Removed                                                    | Replaced with ``SUNErrCode``        |\r\n|:-----------------------------------------|:-------------------------------------|\r\n| `SUNLS_SUCCESS`                                  | `SUN_SUCCESS`                               |\r\n| `SUNLS_UNRECOV_FAILURE`                  | no replacement (value was unused)  |\r\n| `SUNLS_MEM_NULL`                               | `SUN_ERR_ARG_CORRUPT`             |\r\n| `SUNLS_ILL_INPUT`                                 | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                            |\r\n| `SUNLS_MEM_FAIL`                                 | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                     |\r\n| `SUNLS_PACKAGE_FAIL_UNREC`           | `SUN_ERR_EXT_FAIL`                       |\r\n| `SUNLS_VECTOROP_ERR`                       | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                         |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_SUCCESS`                             | `SUN_SUCCESS`                               |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_MEM_NULL`                          | `SUN_ERR_ARG_CORRUPT`             |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_MEM_FAIL`                            | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                     |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_ILL_INPUT`                            | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                           |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_VECTOROP_ERR`                   | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                        |\r\n| `SUN_NLS_EXT_FAIL`                              | `SUN_ERR_EXT_FAIL`                      |\r\n| `SUNMAT_SUCCESS`                               | `SUN_SUCCESS`                              |\r\n| `SUNMAT_ILL_INPUT`                              | `SUN_ERR_ARG_*`                           |\r\n| `SUNMAT_MEM_FAIL`                              | `SUN_ERR_MEM_FAIL`                    |\r\n| `SUNMAT_OPERATION_FAIL`                   | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                       |\r\n| `SUNMAT_MATVEC_SETUP_REQUIRED` | `SUN_ERR_OP_FAIL`                       |\r\n\r\nThe following functions have had their signature updated to ensure they can leverage the new SUNDIALS error handling capabilities.\r\n\r\n```c\r\n// From sundials_futils.h\r\nSUNDIALSFileOpen\r\nSUNDIALSFileClose\r\n\r\n// From sundials_memory.h\r\nSUNMemorNewEmpty\r\nSUNMemoryHelper_Alias\r\nSUNMemoryHelper_Wrap\r\n\r\n// From sundials_nvector.h\r\nN_VNewVectorArray\r\n```\r\n\r\n#### SUNComm Type Added\r\n\r\nWe have replaced the use of a type-erased (i.e., `void*`) pointer to a communicator in place of `MPI_Comm` throughout the SUNDIALS API with a `SUNComm`, which is just a typedef to an `int` in builds without MPI and a typedef to a `MPI_Comm` in builds with MPI. As a result:\r\n\r\n- All users will need to update their codes because the call to `SUNContext_Create` now takes a `SUNComm` instead of type-erased pointer to a communicator. For non-MPI codes, pass `SUN_COMM_NULL` to the `comm` argument instead of `NULL`. For MPI codes, pass the `MPI_Comm` directly.\r\n\r\n- The same change must be made for calls to `SUNLogger_Create` or `SUNProfiler_Create`.\r\n\r\n- Some users will need to update their calls to `N_VGetCommunicator`, and update any custom `N_Vector` implementations that provide `N_VGetCommunicator`, since it now returns a `SUNComm`.\r\n\r\nThe change away from type-erased pointers for `SUNComm` fixes problems like the one described in [GitHub Issue #275](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/275).\r\n\r\nThe SUNLogger is now always MPI-aware if MPI is enabled in SUNDIALS and the `SUNDIALS_LOGGING_ENABLE_MPI` CMake option and macro definition were removed accordingly.\r\n\r\n#### SUNDIALS Core Library\r\n\r\nUsers now need to link to `sundials_core` in addition to the libraries already linked to. This will be picked up automatically in projects that use the SUNDIALS CMake target. The library `sundials_generic` has been superseded by `sundials_core` and is no longer available. This fixes some duplicate symbol errors on Windows when linking to multiple SUNDIALS libraries.\r\n\r\n### Deprecation notice\r\n\r\nThe functions in `sundials_math.h` will be deprecated in the next release.\r\n\r\n```c\r\n  sunrealtype SUNRpowerI(sunrealtype base, int exponent);\r\n  sunrealtype SUNRpowerR(sunrealtype base, sunrealtype exponent);\r\n  sunbooleantype SUNRCompare(sunrealtype a, sunrealtype b);\r\n  sunbooleantype SUNRCompareTol(sunrealtype a, sunrealtype b, sunrealtype tol);\r\n  sunrealtype SUNStrToReal(const char* str);\r\n```\r\n\r\nAdditionally, the following header files (and everything in them) will be deprecated -- users who rely on these are recommended to transition to the corresponding `SUNMatrix` and `SUNLinearSolver` modules:\r\n\r\n```\r\nsundials_direct.h\r\nsundials_dense.h\r\nsundials_band.h\r\n```"}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/134369134", "assets_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v6.7.0", "body": "Added the `SUNAdaptController` base class, ported ARKODE's internal implementations of time step controllers into implementations of this class, and updated ARKODE to use these objects instead of its own implementations. Added `ARKStepSetAdaptController` and `ERKStepSetAdaptController` routines so that users can modify controller parameters, or even provide custom implementations.\r\n\r\nAdded the routines `ARKStepSetAdaptivityAdjustment` and `ERKStepSetAdaptivityAdjustment`, that allow users to adjust the value for the method order supplied to the temporal adaptivity controllers. The ARKODE default for this adjustment has been -1 since its initial release, but for some applications a value of 0 is more appropriate. Users who notice that their simulations encounter a large number of temporal error test failures may want to experiment with adjusting this value.\r\n\r\nAdded the third order ERK method `ARKODE_SHU_OSHER_3_2_3`, the fourth order ERK method `ARKODE_SOFRONIOU_SPALETTA_5_3_4`, the sixth order ERK method `ARKODE_VERNER_9_5_6`, the seventh order ERK method `ARKODE_VERNER_10_6_7`, the eighth order ERK method `ARKODE_VERNER_13_7_8`, and the ninth order ERK method `ARKODE_VERNER_16_8_9`.\r\n\r\nARKStep, ERKStep, MRIStep, and SPRKStep were updated to remove a potentially unnecessary right-hand side evaluation at the end of an integration. ARKStep was additionally updated to remove extra right-hand side evaluations when using an explicit method or an implicit method with an explicit first stage.\r\n\r\nImproved computational complexity of `SUNMatScaleAddI_Sparse` from `O(M*N)` to `O(NNZ)`.\r\n\r\nAdded Fortran support for the LAPACK dense `SUNLinearSolver` implementation.\r\n\r\nFixed a regression introduced by the stop time bug fix in v6.6.1 where ARKODE, CVODE, CVODES, IDA, and IDAS would return at the stop time rather than the requested output time if the stop time was reached in the same step in which the output time was passed.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in ERKStep where methods with `c[s-1] = 1` but `a[s-1,j] != b[j]` were incorrectly treated as having the first same as last (FSAL) property.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in ARKODE where `ARKStepSetInterpolateStopTime` would return an interpolated solution at the stop time in some cases when interpolation was disabled.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in `ARKStepSetTableNum` wherein it did not recognize `ARKODE_ARK2_ERK_3_1_2` and `ARKODE_ARK2_DIRK_3_1_2` as a valid additive Runge--Kutta Butcher table pair.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in `MRIStepCoupling_Write` where explicit coupling tables were not written to the output file pointer.\r\n\r\nThe `MRIStepInnerStepper` class in MRIStep was updated to make supplying an `MRIStepInnerFullRhsFn` optional.\r\n\r\nFixed scaling bug in `SUNMatScaleAddI_Sparse` for non-square matrices.\r\n\r\nChanged the `SUNProfiler` so that it does not rely on `MPI_WTime` in any case. This fixes [GitHub Issue #312](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/issues/312).\r\n\r\nFixed missing soversions in some `SUNLinearSolver` and `SUNNonlinearSolver` CMake targets.\r\n\r\nRenamed some internal types in CVODES and IDAS to allow both packages to be built together in the same binary.", "reactions": {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/134369134/reactions", "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v6.6.0", "body": "A new time-stepping module, `SPRKStep`, was added to ARKODE. This time-stepper provides explicit symplectic partitioned Runge-Kutta methods up to order 10 for separable Hamiltonian systems.\r\n\r\nAdded support for relaxation Runge-Kutta methods to ERKStep and ARKStep in ARKODE.\r\n\r\nAdded the second order IMEX method from Giraldo, Kelly, and Constantinescu 2013 as the default second order IMEX method in ARKStep. The explicit table is given by `ARKODE_ARK2_ERK_3_1_2` and the implicit table by `ARKODE_ARK2_DIRK_3_1_2`.\r\n\r\nUpdated CVODE, CVODES and ARKODE default behavior when returning the solution when the internal time has reached a user-specified stop time.  Previously, the output solution was interpolated to the value of `tstop`; the default is now to copy the internal solution vector.  Users who wish to revert to interpolation may call a new routine `CVodeSetInterpolateStopTime`, `ARKStepSetInterpolateStopTime`, `ERKStepSetInterpolateStopTime`, or `MRIStepSetInterpolateStopTime`.\r\n\r\nA potential bug was fixed when using inequality constraint handling and calling `ARKStepGetEstLocalErrors` or `ERKStepGetEstLocalErrors` after a failed step in which an inequality constraint violation occurred. In this case, the values returned by `ARKStepGetEstLocalErrors` or `ERKStepGetEstLocalErrors` may have been invalid.\r\n\r\nUpdated the F2003 utility routines `SUNDIALSFileOpen` and Numer. Math., 146, 2019] to\r\nARKODE.\r\n\r\nFixed the unituitive behavior of the `USE_GENERIC_MATH` CMake option which\r\ncaused the double precision math functions to be used regardless of the value of\r\n`SUNDIALS_PRECISION`. "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v6.2.0", "body": "**https://github.com/LLNL/sundials is now the official SUNDIALS development repository**.\r\n\r\nAdded the `SUNLogger` API which provides a SUNDIALS-wide\r\nmechanism for logging of errors, warnings, informational output,\r\nand debugging output.\r\n\r\nDeprecated the following functions, it is recommended to use the `SUNLogger` API\r\ninstead.\r\n\r\n* `ARKStepSetDiagnostics`\r\n* `ERKStepSetDiagnostics`\r\n* `MRIStepSetDiagnostics`\r\n* `KINSetInfoFile`\r\n* `SUNNonlinSolSetPrintLevel_Newton`\r\n* `SUNNonlinSolSetInfoFile_Newton`\r\n* `SUNNonlinSolSetPrintLevel_FixedPoint`\r\n* `SUNNonlinSolSetInfoFile_FixedPoint`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_PCG`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetPrintLevel_PCG`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_SPGMR`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetPrintLevel_SPGMR`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_SPFGMR`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetPrintLevel_SPFGMR`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_SPTFQM`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetPrintLevel_SPTFQMR`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_SPBCGS`\r\n* `SUNLinSolSetPrintLevel_SPBCGS`\r\n\r\nThe `SUNLinSolSetInfoFile_**` and  `SUNNonlinSolSetInfoFile_*` family of\r\nfunctions are now enabled by setting the CMake option `SUNDIALS_LOGGING_LEVEL`\r\nto a value `>= 3`.\r\n\r\nAdded the function `SUNProfiler_Reset` to reset the region timings and counters\r\nto zero.\r\n\r\nAdded the functions `ARKStepPrintAllStats`, `ERKStepPrintAllStats`,\r\n`MRIStepPrintAll`, `CVodePrintAllStats`, `IDAPrintAllStats`, and\r\n`KINPrintAllStats` to output all of the integrator, nonlinear solver, linear\r\nsolver, and other statistics in one call. The file `scripts/sundials_csv.py`\r\ncontains functions for parsing the comma-separated value output files.\r\n\r\nAdded functions to CVODE, CVODES, IDA, and IDAS to change the default step size\r\nadaptivity parameters. For more information see the documentation for:\r\n\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaFixedStepBounds`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMaxFirstStep`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMaxEarlyStep`\r\n* `CVodeSetNumStepsEtaMaxEarlyStep`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMax`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMin`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMinErrFailEta`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaMaxErrFailEta`\r\n* `CVodeSetNumFailsEtaMaxErrFail`\r\n* `CVodeSetEtaConvFail`\r\n* `IDASetEtaFixedStepBounds`\r\n* `IDAsetEtaMax`\r\n* `IDASetEtaMin`\r\n* `IDASetEtaLow`\r\n* `IDASetEtaMinErrFail`\r\n* `IDASetEtaConvFail`\r\n\r\nAdded the functions `CVodeSetDeltaGammaMaxLSetup` and\r\n`CVodeSetDeltaGammaMaxBadJac` in CVODE and CVODES to adjust the `gamma` change\r\nthresholds to require a linear solver setup or Jacobian/precondition update,\r\nrespectively.\r\n\r\nAdded the function `IDASetDetlaCjLSetup` in IDA and IDAS to adjust the parameter\r\nthat determines when a change in `c_j` requires calling the linear solver setup\r\nfunction.\r\n\r\nAdded the function `MRIStepSetOrder` to select the default MRI method of a given\r\norder.\r\n\r\nAdded support to CVODES for integrating IVPs with constraints using BDF methods\r\nand projecting the solution onto the constraint manifold with a user defined\r\nprojection function. This implementation is accompanied by additions to the\r\nCVODES user documentation and examples.\r\n\r\nThe behavior of `N_VSetKernelExecPolicy_Sycl` has been updated to be consistent\r\nwith the CUDA and HIP vectors. The input execution policies are now cloned and\r\nmay be freed after calling `N_VSetKernelExecPolicy_Sycl`. Additionally, `NULL`\r\ninputs are now allowed and, if provided, will reset the vector execution\r\npolicies to the defaults.\r\n\r\nFixed the `SUNContext` convenience class for C++ users to disallow copy\r\nconstruction and allow move construction.\r\n\r\nA memory leak in the SYCL vector was fixed where the execution policies were\r\nnot freed when the vector was destroyed.\r\n\r\nThe include guard in `nvector_mpimanyvector.h` has been corrected to enable\r\nusing both the ManyVector and MPIManyVector NVector implementations in the same\r\nsimulation.\r\n\r\nChanged exported SUNDIALS PETSc CMake targets to be INTERFACE IMPORTED instead\r\nof UNKNOWN IMPORTED.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in the integrator functions to retrieve the number of nonlinear\r\nsolver failures. The failure count returned was the number of failed *steps* due\r\nto a nonlinear solver failure i.e., if a nonlinear solve failed with a stale\r\nJacobian or preconditioner but succeeded after updating the Jacobian or\r\npreconditioner, the initial failure was not included in the nonlinear solver\r\nfailure count. The following functions have been updated to return the total\r\nnumber of nonlinear solver failures:\r\n\r\n* `ARKStepGetNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `ARKStepGetNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `MRIStepGetNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `MRIStepGetNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `CVodeGetNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `CVodeGetSensNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetSensNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `CVodeGetStgrSensNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetStgrSensNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `IDAGetNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `IDAGetNonlinSolvStats`\r\n* `IDAGetSensNumNonlinSolvConvFails`\r\n* `IDAGetSensNonlinSolvStats`\r\n\r\nAs such users may see an increase in the number of failures reported from the\r\nabove functions. The following functions have been added to retrieve the number\r\nof failed steps due to a nonlinear solver failure i.e., the counts previously\r\nreturned by the above functions:\r\n\r\n* `ARKStepGetNumStepSolveFails`\r\n* `MRIStepGetNumStepSolveFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetNumStepSolveFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetNumStepSensSolveFails`\r\n* `CVodeGetNumStepStgrSensSolveFails`\r\n* "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v6.0.0", "body": "## Changes to SUNDIALS in release 6.0.0\r\n\r\n### SUNContext\r\n\r\nSUNDIALS v6.0.0 introduces a new `SUNContext` object on which all other SUNDIALS\r\nobjects depend. As such, the constructors for all SUNDIALS packages, vectors,\r\nmatrices, linear solvers, nonlinear solvers, and memory helpers have been\r\nupdated to accept a context as the last input. Users upgrading to SUNDIALS\r\nv6.0.0 will need to call `SUNContext_Create` to create a context object with\r\nbefore calling any other SUNDIALS library function, and then provide this object\r\nto other SUNDIALS constructors. The context object has been introduced to allow\r\nSUNDIALS to provide new features, such as the profiling/instrumentation also\r\nintroduced in this release, while maintaining thread-safety. See the\r\ndocumentation section on the `SUNContext` for more details.\r\n\r\nA script [upgrade-to-sundials-6-from-5.sh](https://github.com/LLNL/sundials/releases/download/v6.0.0/upgrade-to-sundials-6-from-5.sh) has been provided with the release\r\n(obtainable from the GitHub release page) to help ease the transition to\r\nSUNDIALS v6.0.0. The script will add a `SUNCTX_PLACEHOLDER` argument to all of\r\nthe calls to SUNDIALS constructors that now require a `SUNContext` object. It\r\ncan also update deprecated SUNDIALS constants/types to the new names. It can be\r\nrun like this:\r\n\r\n```\r\n> ./upgrade-to-sundials-6-from-5.sh <files to update>\r\n```\r\n\r\n### SUNProfiler\r\n\r\nA capability to profile/instrument SUNDIALS library code has been added. This\r\ncan be enabled with the CMake option `SUNDIALS_BUILD_WITH_PROFILING`. A built-in\r\nprofiler will be used by default, but the\r\n[Caliper](https://github.com/LLNL/Caliper) library can also be used instead with\r\nthe CMake option `ENABLE_CALIPER`. See the documentation section on profiling\r\nfor more details.  **WARNING**: Profiling will impact performance, and should be\r\nenabled judiciously.\r\n\r\n### SUNMemoryHelper\r\n\r\nThe `SUNMemoryHelper` functions `Alloc`, `Dealloc`, and `Copy` have been updated\r\nto accept an opaque handle as the last input. At a minimum, existing\r\n`SUNMemoryHelper` implementations will need to update these functions to accept\r\nthe additional argument. Typically, this handle is the execution stream (e.g., a\r\nCUDA/HIP stream or SYCL queue) for the operation. The CUDA, HIP, and SYCL\r\n`SUNMemoryHelper` implementations have been updated accordingly. Additionally,\r\nthe constructor for the SYCL implementation has been updated to remove the SYCL\r\nqueue as an input.\r\n\r\n### NVector\r\n\r\nTwo new optional vector operations, `N_VDotProdMultiLocal` and\r\n`N_VDotProdMultiAllReduce`, have been added to support low-synchronization\r\nmethods for Anderson acceleration.\r\n\r\nThe CUDA, HIP, and SYCL execution policies have been moved from the `sundials`\r\nnamespace to the `sundials::cuda`, `sundials::hip`, and `sundials::sycl`\r\nnamespaces respectively. Accordingly, the prefixes \"Cuda\", \"Hip\", and \"Sycl\"\r\nhave been removed from the execution policy classes and methods.\r\n\r\nThe `Sundials` namespace used by the Trilinos Tpetra NVector has been replaced\r\nwith the `sundials::trilinos::nvector_tpetra` namespace.\r\n\r\nThe serial, PThreads, PETSc, *hypre*, Parallel, OpenMP_DEV, and OpenMP vector\r\nfunctions `N_VCloneVectorArray_*` and `N_VDestroyVectorArray_*` have been\r\ndeprecated. The generic `N_VCloneVectorArray` and `N_VDestroyVectorArray`\r\nfunctions should be used instead.\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated constructor `N_VMakeWithManagedAllocator_Cuda` and\r\nthe function `N_VSetCudaStream_Cuda` have been removed and replaced with\r\n`N_VNewWithMemHelp_Cuda` and `N_VSetKerrnelExecPolicy_Cuda` respectively.\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated macros `PVEC_REAL_MPI_TYPE` and\r\n`PVEC_INTEGER_MPI_TYPE` have been removed and replaced with\r\n`MPI_SUNREALTYPE` and `MPI_SUNINDEXTYPE` respectively.\r\n\r\n### SUNLinearSolver\r\n\r\nThe following previously deprecated functions have been removed\r\n\r\n| Removed                   | Replaced with                    |\r\n|:--------------------------|:---------------------------------|\r\n| `SUNBandLinearSolver`     | `SUNLinSol_Band`                 |\r\n| `SUNDenseLinearSolver`    | `SUNLinSol_Dense`                |\r\n| `SUNKLU`                  | `SUNLinSol_KLU`                  |\r\n| `SUNKLUReInit`            | `SUNLinSol_KLUReInit`            |\r\n| `SUNKLUSetOrdering`       | `SUNLinSol_KLUSetOrdering`       |\r\n| `SUNLapackBand`           | `SUNLinSol_LapackBand`           |\r\n| `SUNLapackDense`          | `SUNLinSol_LapackDense`          |\r\n| `SUNPCG`                  | `SUNLinSol_PCG`                  |\r\n| `SUNPCGSetPrecType`       | `SUNLinSol_PCGSetPrecType`       |\r\n| `SUNPCGSetMaxl`           | `SUNLinSol_PCGSetMaxl`           |\r\n| `SUNSPBCGS`               | `SUNLinSol_SPBCGS`               |\r\n| `SUNSPBCGSSetPrecType`    | `SUNLinSol_SPBCGSSetPrecType`    |\r\n| `SUNSPBCGSSetMaxl`        | `SUNLinSol_SPBCGSSetMaxl`        |\r\n| `SUNSPFGMR`               | `SUNLinSol_SPFGMR`               |\r\n| `SUNSPFGMRSetPrecType`    | `SUNLinSol_SPFGMRSetPrecType`    |\r\n| `SUNSPFGMRSetGSType`      | `SUNLinSol_SPFGMRSetGSType`      |\r\n| `SUNSPFGMRSetMaxRestarts` | `SUNLinSol_SPFGMRSetMaxRestarts` |\r\n| `SUNSPGMR`                | `SUNLinSol_SPGMR`                |\r\n| `SUNSPGMRSetPrecType`     | `SUNLinSol_SPGMRSetPrecType`     |\r\n| `SUNSPGMRSetGSType`       | `SUNLinSol_SPGMRSetGSType`       |\r\n| `SUNSPGMRSetMaxRestarts`  | `SUNLinSol_SPGMRSetMaxRestarts`  |\r\n| `SUNSPTFQMR`              | `SUNLinSol_SPTFQMR`              |\r\n| `SUNSPTFQMRSetPrecType`   | `SUNLinSol_SPTFQMRSetPrecType`   |\r\n| `SUNSPTFQMRSetMaxl`       | `SUNLinSol_SPTFQMRSetMaxl`       |\r\n| `SUNSuperLUMT`            | `SUNLinSol_SuperLUMT`            |\r\n| `SUNSuperLUMTSetOrdering` | `SUNLinSol_SuperLUMTSetOrdering` |\r\n\r\n### Fortran Interfaces\r\n\r\nThe ARKODE, CVODE, IDA, and KINSOL Fortran 77 interfaces have been removed. See\r\nthe \"SUNDIALS Fortran Interface\" section in the user guides and the F2003\r\nexample programs for more details using the SUNDIALS Fortran 2003 module\r\ninterfaces.\r\n\r\n### ARKODE\r\n\r\nThe ARKODE MRIStep module has been extended to support implicit-explicit (IMEX)\r\nmultirate infinitesimal generalized additive Runge-Kutta (MRI-GARK) methods. As\r\nsuch, `MRIStepCreate` has been updated to include arguments for the slow\r\nexplicit and slow implicit ODE right-hand side functions. `MRIStepCreate` has\r\nalso been updated to require attaching an `MRIStepInnerStepper` for evolving the\r\nfast time scale. `MRIStepReInit` has been similarly updated to take explicit\r\nand implicit right-hand side functions as input. Codes using explicit or\r\nimplicit MRI methods will need to update `MRIStepCreate` and `MRIStepReInit`\r\ncalls to pass `NULL` for either the explicit or implicit right-hand side\r\nfunction as appropriate. If ARKStep is used as the fast time scale integrator,\r\ncodes will need to call `ARKStepCreateMRIStepInnerStepper` to wrap the ARKStep\r\nmemory as an `MRIStepInnerStepper` object. Additionally, `MRIStepGetNumRhsEvals`\r\nhas been updated to return the number of slow implicit and explicit function\r\nevaluations. The coupling table structure `MRIStepCouplingMem` and the\r\nfunctions `MRIStepCoupling_Alloc` and `MRIStepCoupling_Create` have also\r\nbeen updated to support IMEX-MRI-GARK methods.\r\n\r\nThe deprecated functions `MRIStepGetCurrentButcherTables` and\r\n`MRIStepWriteButcher` and the utility functions `MRIStepSetTable` and\r\n`MRIStepSetTableNum` have been removed. Users wishing to create an MRI-GARK\r\nmethod from a Butcher table should use `MRIStepCoupling_MIStoMRI` to create\r\nthe corresponding MRI coupling table and attach it with `MRIStepSetCoupling`.\r\n\r\nThe implementation of solve-decoupled implicit MRI-GARK methods has been updated\r\nto remove extraneous slow implicit function calls and reduce the memory\r\nrequirements.\r\n\r\nDeprecated ARKODE nonlinear solver predictors: specification of the ARKStep\r\n\"bootstrap\" or \"minimum correction\" predictors (options 4 and 5 from\r\n`ARKStepSetPredictorMethod`), or MRIStep \"bootstrap\" predictor (option 4 from\r\n`MRIStepSetPredictorMethod`), will output a deprecation warning message.\r\nThese options will be removed in a future release.\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated functions `ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenLSet` and\r\n`ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` have been removed and replaced with\r\n`ARKStepSetLSetupFrequency` and `ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` respectively.\r\n\r\n### CVODE\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated function `CVodeSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` has been removed\r\nand replaced with `CVodeSetJacEvalFrequency`.\r\n\r\n### CVODES\r\n\r\nAdded a new function `CVodeGetLinSolveStats` to get the CVODES linear solver\r\nstatistics as a group.\r\n\r\nAdded a new function, `CVodeSetMonitorFn`, that takes a user-function\r\nto be called by CVODES after every `nst` successfully completed time-steps.\r\nThis is intended to provide a way of monitoring the CVODES statistics\r\nthroughout the simulation.\r\n\r\nThe previously deprecated function `CVodeSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` has been removed\r\nand replaced with `CVodeSetJacEvalFrequency`.\r\n\r\n### KINSOL\r\n\r\nNew orthogonalization methods were added for use within Anderson acceleration\r\nin KINSOL. See the \"Anderson Acceleration QR Factorization\" subsection within\r\nthe mathematical considerations chapter of the user guide and the\r\n`KINSetOrthAA` function documentation for more details.\r\n\r\n### Deprecations\r\n\r\nIn addition to the deprecations noted elsewhere, many constants, types, and\r\nfunctions have been renamed so that they are properly namespaced. The old names\r\nhave been deprecated and will be removed in SUNDIALS v7.0.0.\r\n\r\nThe following constants, macros, and  typedefs are now deprecated:\r\n\r\n| Deprecated Name            | New Name                          |\r\n|:---------------------------|:----------------------------------|\r\n| `realtype`                 | `sunrealtype`                     |\r\n| `booleantype`              | `sunbooleantype`                  |\r\n| `RCONST`                   | `SUN_RCONST`                      |\r\n| `BIG_REAL`                 | `SUN_BIG_REAL`                    |\r\n| `SMALL_REAL`               | `SUN_SMALL_REAL`                  |\r\n| `UNIT_ROUNDOFF`            | `SUN_UNIT_ROUNDOFF`               |\r\n| `PREC_NONE`                | `SUN_PREC_NONE`                   |\r\n| `PREC_LEFT`                | `SUN_PREC_LEFT`                   |\r\n| `PREC_RIGHT`               | `SUN_PREC_RIGHT`                  |\r\n| `PREC_BOTH`                | `SUN_PREC_BOTH`                   |\r\n| `MODIFIED_GS`              | `SUN_MODIFIED_GS`                 |\r\n| `CLASSICAL_GS`             | `SUN_CLASSICAL_GS`                |\r\n| `ATimesFn`                 | `SUNATimesFn` `SUNDLS_BAND_COL`                 |\r\n| `BAND_COL_ELEM`            | `SUNDLS_BAND_COL_ELEM`            |\r\n| `BAND_ELEM`                | `SUNDLS_BAND_ELEM`                |\r\n| `SDIRK_2_1_2` "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v5.8.0", "body": "# Changes to SUNDIALS in release 5.8.0\r\n\r\nThe RAJA NVECTOR implementation has been updated to support the SYCL backend in addition to the CUDA and HIP backend. Users can choose the backend when configuring SUNDIALS by using the `SUNDIALS_RAJA_BACKENDS` CMake variable. This module remains experimental and is subject to change from version to version.\r\n\r\nA new SUNMatrix and SUNLinearSolver implementation were added to interface with the Intel oneAPI Math Kernel Library (oneMKL). Both the matrix and the linear solver support general dense linear systems as well as block diagonal linear systems. This module is experimental and is subject to change from version to version.\r\n\r\nAdded a new *optional* function to the SUNLinearSolver API, `SUNLinSolSetZeroGuess`, to indicate that the next call to `SUNlinSolSolve` will be made with a zero initial guess. SUNLinearSolver implementations that do not use the `SUNLinSolNewEmpty` constructor will, at a minimum, need set the ``setzeroguess`` function pointer in the linear solver ``ops`` structure to ``NULL``. The SUNDIALS iterative linear solver implementations have been updated to leverage this new set function to remove one dot product per solve.\r\n\r\nThe time integrator packages (ARKODE, CVODE(S), and IDA(S)) all now support a new \"matrix-embedded\" SUNLinearSolver type.  This type supports user-supplied SUNLinearSolver implementations that set up and solve the specified linear system at each linear solve call.  Any matrix-related data structures are held internally to the linear solver itself, and are not provided by the SUNDIALS package.\r\n\r\nAdded functions to ARKODE and CVODE(S) for supplying an alternative right-hand side function and to IDA(S) for supplying an alternative residual for use within nonlinear system function evaluations.\r\n\r\nSupport for user-defined inner (fast) integrators has been to the MRIStep module in ARKODE. See the \"MRIStep Custom Inner Steppers\" section in the user guide for more information on providing a user-defined integration method.\r\n\r\nAdded specialized fused HIP kernels to CVODE which may offer better performance on smaller problems when using CVODE with the `NVECTOR_HIP` module. See the optional input function `CVodeSetUseIntegratorFusedKernels` for more information. As with other SUNDIALS HIP features, this is feature is experimental and may change from version to version.\r\n\r\nNew KINSOL options have been added to apply a constant damping factor in the fixed point and Picard iterations (see `KINSetDamping`), to delay the start of Anderson acceleration with the fixed point and Picard iterations (see `KINSetDelayAA`), and to return the newest solution with the fixed point iteration (see `KINSetReturnNewest`).\r\n\r\nThe installed SUNDIALSConfig.cmake file now supports the `COMPONENTS` option to `find_package`. The exported targets no longer have `IMPORTED_GLOBAL` set.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in ``SUNMatCopyOps`` where the matrix-vector product setup function pointer was not copied.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in the SPBCGS and SPTFQMR solvers for the case where a non-zero initial guess and a solution scaling vector are provided. This fix only impacts codes using SPBCGS or SPTFQMR as standalone solvers as all SUNDIALS packages utilize a zero initial guess.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in the ARKODE stepper modules where the stop time may be passed after resetting the integrator.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in `IDASetJacTimesResFn` in IDAS where the supplied function was used in the dense finite difference Jacobian computation rather than the finite difference Jacobian-vector product approximation.\r\n\r\nA bug was fixed in the KINSOL Picard iteration where the value of `KINSetMaxSetupCalls` would be ignored.\r\n", Users can choose the backend when configuring\r\nSUNDIALS by using the `SUNDIALS_RAJA_BACKENDS` CMake variable. This module\r\nremains experimental and is subject to change from version to version.\r\n\r\nA new optional operation, `N_VGetDeviceArrayPointer`, was added to the N_Vector\r\nAPI. This operation is useful for N_Vectors that utilize dual memory spaces,\r\ne.g. the native SUNDIALS CUDA N_Vector.\r\n\r\nThe SUNMATRIX_CUSPARSE and SUNLINEARSOLVER_CUSOLVERSP_BATCHQR implementations\r\nno longer require the SUNDIALS CUDA N_Vector. Instead, they require that the vector\r\nutilized provides the `N_VGetDeviceArrayPointer` operation, and that the pointer\r\nreturned by `N_VGetDeviceArrayPointer` is a valid CUDA device pointer."}, "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v5.4.0", "body": "## Changes to SUNDIALS in release 5.4.0\r\n\r\nAdded full support for time-dependent mass matrices in ARKStep, and expanded\r\nexisting non-identity mass matrix infrastructure to support use of the\r\nfixed point nonlinear solver.  Fixed bug for ERK method integration with\r\nstatic mass matrices.\r\n\r\nAn interface between ARKStep and the XBraid multigrid reduction in time (MGRIT)\r\nlibrary has been added to enable parallel-in-time integration. See the ARKStep\r\ndocumentation and examples for more details. This interface required the\r\naddition of three new N_Vector operations to exchange vector data between\r\ncomputational nodes, see `N_VBufSize`, `N_VBufPack`, and `N_VBufUnpack`. These\r\nN_Vector operations are only used within the XBraid interface and need not be\r\nimplemented for any other context.\r\n\r\nUpdated the MRIStep time-stepping module in ARKode to support\r\nhigher-order MRI-GARK methods [Sandu, SIAM J. Numer. Anal., 57, 2019],\r\nincluding methods that involve solve-decoupled, diagonally-implicit\r\ntreatment of the slow time scale.\r\n\r\nA new API, `SUNMemoryHelper`, was added to support **GPU users** who have complex\r\nmemory management needs such as using memory pools. This is paired with new\r\nconstructors for the `NVECTOR_CUDA` and `NVECTOR_RAJA` modules that accept a\r\n`SUNMemoryHelper` object. Refer to \"The SUNMemoryHelper API\", \"NVECTOR CUDA\"\r\nand \"NVECTOR RAJA\" sections in the documentation for more information.\r\n\r\nThe `NVECTOR_RAJA` module has been updated to mirror the `NVECTOR_CUDA` module.\r\nNotably, the update adds managed memory support to the `NVECTOR_RAJA` module.\r\nUsers of the module will need to update any calls to the `N_VMake_Raja` function\r\nbecause that signature was changed. This module remains experimental and is\r\nsubject to change from version to version.\r\n\r\nAdded new `SetLSNormFactor()` functions to CVODE(S), ARKODE, and IDA(S) to\r\nto specify the factor for converting between integrator tolerances (WRMS norm)\r\nand linear solver tolerances (L2 norm) i.e., `tol_L2 = nrmfac * tol_WRMS`.\r\n\r\nAdded new reset functions `ARKStepReset()`, `ERKStepReset()`, and\r\n`MRIStepReset()` to reset the stepper time and state vector to user-provided\r\nvalues for continuing the integration from that point while retaining the\r\nintegration history. These function complement the reinitialization functions\r\n`ARKStepReInit()`, `ERKStepReInit()`, and `MRIStepReInit()` which reinitialize\r\nthe stepper so that the problem integration should resume as if started from\r\nscratch.\r\n\r\nAdded new functions for advanced users providing a custom `SUNNonlinSolSysFn`.\r\n\r\nThe expected behavior of `SUNNonlinSolGetNumIters` and\r\n`SUNNonlinSolGetNumConvFails` in the SUNNonlinearSolver API have been updated to\r\nspecify that they should return the number of nonlinear solver iterations and\r\nconvergence failures in the most recent solve respectively rather than the\r\ncumulative number of iterations and failures across all solves respectively. The\r\nAPI documentation and SUNDIALS provided SUNNonlinearSolver implementations and\r\nhave been updated accordingly. As before, the cumulative number of nonlinear\r\niterations and failures may be retreived by calling the integrator provided get\r\nfunctions.\r\n\r\n**This change may cause a runtime error in existing user code**.\r\nIn IDAS and CVODES, the functions for forward integration with checkpointing\r\n(`IDASolveF`, `CVodeF`) are now subject to a restriction on the number of time\r\nsteps allowed to reach the output time. This is the same restriction applied to\r\nthe `IDASolve` and `CVode` functions. The default maximum number of steps is\r\n500, but this may be changed using the `<IDA|CVode>SetMaxNumSteps` function.\r\nThis change fixes a bug that could cause an infinite loop in the `IDASolveF`\r\nand `CVodeF` and functions.\r\n\r\nA minor inconsistency in CVODE(S) and a bug ARKODE when checking the Jacobian\r\nevaluation frequency has been fixed. As a result codes using using a\r\nnon-default Jacobian update frequency through a call to\r\n`CVodeSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` or `ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenJac` will need to\r\nincrease the provided value by 1 to achieve the same behavior as before. For\r\ngreater clarity the functions `CVodeSetMaxStepsBetweenJac`,\r\n`ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenJac`, and `ARKStepSetMaxStepsBetweenLSet` have been\r\ndeprecated and replaced with `CVodeSetJacEvalFrequency`,\r\n`ARKStepSetJacEvalFrequency`, and `ARKStepSetLSetupFrequency` respectively.\r\nAdditionally, the function `CVodeSetLSetupFrequency` has been added to CVODE(S)\r\nto set the frequency of calls to the linear solver setup function.\r\n\r\nThe `NVECTOR_TRILINOS` module has been updated to work with Trilinos 12.18+.\r\nThis update changes the local ordinal type to always be an `int`.\r\n\r\nAdded support for CUDA v11."}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/26738227", "assets_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v5.3.0", "body": "## Changes to SUNDIALS in release 5.3.0\r\n\r\nAdded support to CVODE for integrating IVPs with constraints using BDF methods\r\nand projecting the solution onto the constraint manifold with a user defined\r\nprojection function. This implementation is accompanied by additions to the\r\nCVODE user documentation and examples.\r\n\r\nAdded the ability to control the CUDA kernel launch parameters for the\r\n`NVECTOR_CUDA` and `SUNMATRIX_CUSPARSE` modules. These modules remain\r\nexperimental and are subject to change from version to version.\r\nIn addition, the `NVECTOR_CUDA` kernels were rewritten to be more flexible.\r\nMost users should see equivalent performance or some improvement, but a select\r\nfew may observe minor performance degradation with the default settings. Users\r\nare encouraged to contact the SUNDIALS team about any perfomance changes\r\nthat they notice.\r\n\r\nAdded new capabilities for monitoring the solve phase in the `SUNNONLINSOL_NEWTON`\r\nand `SUNNONLINSOL_FIXEDPOINT` modules, and the SUNDIALS iterative linear solver\r\nmodules. SUNDIALS must be built with the CMake option\r\n`SUNDIALS_BUILD_WITH_MONITORING` to use these capabilities.\r\n\r\nAdded a new function, `CVodeSetMonitorFn`, that takes a user-function\r\nto be called by CVODE after every `nst` succesfully completed time-steps.\r\nThis is intended to provide a way of monitoring the CVODE statistics\r\nthroughout the simulation.\r\n\r\nAdded specialized fused CUDA kernels to CVODE which may offer better\r\nperformance on smaller problems when using CVODE with the `NVECTOR_CUDA`\r\nmodule. See the optional input function `CVodeSetUseIntegratorFusedKernels`\r\nfor more information. As with other SUNDIALS CUDA features, this feature is experimental\r\nand may change from version to version.\r\n\r\nAdded a new function `CVodeGetLinSolveStats` to get the CVODE linear solver\r\nstatistics as a group.\r\n\r\nAdded optional set functions to provide an alternative ODE right-hand side\r\nfunction (ARKode and CVODE(S)), DAE residual function (IDA(S)), or nonlinear\r\nsystem function (KINSOL) for use when computing Jacobian-vector products with\r\nthe internal difference quotient approximation.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in ARKode where the prototypes for `ERKStepSetMinReduction()` and\r\n`ARKStepSetMinReduction()` were not included in `arkode_erkstep.h` and\r\n`arkode_arkstep.h` respectively.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in ARKode where inequality constraint checking would need to be\r\ndisabled and then re-enabled to update the inequality constraint values after\r\nresizing a problem. Resizing a problem will now disable constraints and a call\r\nto `ARKStepSetConstraints` or `ERKStepSetConstraints` is required to re-enable\r\nconstraint checking for the new problem size.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in the iterative linear solver modules where an error is not\r\nreturned if the Atimes function is `NULL` or, if preconditioning is enabled, the\r\nPSolve function is `NULL`.\r\n\r\n"}, {"url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/25050084", "assets_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/releases/25050084/assets", "upload_url": "https://api.github.com/repos/LLNL/sundials/zipball/v5.2.0", "body": "## Changes to SUNDIALS in release 5.2.0\r\n\r\nFixed a build system bug related to the Fortran 2003 interfaces when using the\r\nIBM XL compiler. When building the Fortran 2003 interfaces with an XL compiler\r\nit is recommended to set `CMAKE_Fortran_COMPILER` to `f2003`, `xlf2003`, or\r\n`xlf2003_r`.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in how ARKode interfaces with a user-supplied, iterative, unscaled linear solver.\r\nIn this case, ARKode adjusts the linear solver tolerance in an attempt to account for the\r\nlack of support for left/right scaling matrices.  Previously, ARKode computed this scaling\r\nfactor using the error weight vector, `ewt`; this fix changes that to the residual weight vector,\r\n\r\nFixed a linkage bug affecting Windows users that stemmed from dllimport/dllexport\r\nattribute missing on some SUNDIALS API functions.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug in how ARKode interfaces with a user-supplied, iterative, unscaled linear solver.\r\nIn this case, ARKode adjusts the linear solver tolerance in an attempt to account for the\r\nlack of support for left/right scaling matrices.  Previously, ARKode computed this scaling\r\nfactor using the error weight vector, `ewt`; this fix changes that to the residual weight vector,\r\n`rwt`, that can differ from `ewt` when solving problems with non-identity mass matrix.\r\n\r\nFixed a similar bug in how ARKode interfaces with scaled linear solvers when solving problems\r\nwith non-identity mass matrices.  Here, the left scaling matrix should correspond with `rwt`\r\nand the right scaling matrix with `ewt`; these were reversed but are now correct.\r\n\r\nFixed a memory leak in CVODES and IDAS from not deallocating the `atolSmin0` and\r\n`atolQSmin0` arrays.\r\n\r\nFixed a bug where a non-default value for the maximum allowed growth factor\r\nafter the first step would be ignored.\r\n\r\nFunctions were added to each of the time integration packages to enable or\r\ndisable the scaling applied to linear system solutions with matrix-based linear solvers\r\nto account for lagged matrix information.\r\n\r\nAdded two new functions, `ARKStepSetMinReduction()` and\r\n`ERKStepSetMinReduction()` to change the minimum allowed step size reduction factor\r\nafter an error test failure.\r\n\r\nAdded a new `SUNMatrix` implementation, `SUNMATRIX_CUSPARSE`, that interfaces\r\nto the sparse matrix implementation from the NVIDIA cuSPARSE library. In addition,\r\nthe `SUNLINSOL_CUSOLVER_BATCHQR` linear solver has been updated to\r\nuse this matrix, therefore, users of this module will need to update their code.\r\nThese modules are still considered to be experimental, thus they are subject to\r\nbreaking changes even in minor releases.\r\n\r\nAdded a new \"stiff\" interpolation module to ARKode, based on Lagrange polynomial interpolation,\r\nthat is accessible to each of the ARKStep, ERKStep and MRIStep time-stepping modules.\r\nThis module is designed to provide increased interpolation accuracy when integrating\r\nstiff problems, as opposed to the ARKode-standard Hermite interpolation module that\r\ncan suffer when the IVP right-hand side has large Lipschitz constant.  While the Hermite module\r\nremains the default, the new Lagrange module may be enabled using one of the routines\r\n`ARKStepSetInterpolantType`, `ERKStepSetInterpolantType`, or `MRIStepSetInterpolantType`.\r\nThe serial example problem ``ark_brusselator.c`` has been converted to use this Lagrange\r\ninterpolation module.  Created accompanying routines `ARKStepSetInterpolantDegree`,\r\n`ARKStepSetInterpolantDegree` and `ARKStepSetInterpolantDegree` to provide user control over\r\nthese interpolating polynomials. While the routines `ARKStepSetDenseOrder`,\r\n`ARKStepSetDenseOrder` and `ARKStepSetDenseOrder` still exist, these have been deprecated and\r\nwill be removed in a future release.\r\n", "reactions":
